        getPathByNewspaper: function (newspaper) {
            for (var i = 0; i < nozGlobal.defaultInfos.length; i++) {
                var newspaperInfo = nozGlobal.defaultInfos[i];
                if (newspaperInfo.name === newspaper || newspaperInfo.acronym === newspaper) {
                    if (!newspaperInfo.isIntern) {
                        return "https://" + newspaperInfo['domain'];
                    }
                    return newspaperInfo.parentSlug + newspaperInfo.slug;
                }
            }
            return nozGlobal.defaultNewspaperConfig.parentSlug + nozGlobal.defaultNewspaperConfig.slug;
        },
        getHostByNewspaper: function (newspaper) {
            for (var i = 0; i < nozGlobal.defaultInfos.length; i++) {
                var newspaperInfo = nozGlobal.defaultInfos[i];
                if (!newspaperInfo.isIntern &&
                        (newspaperInfo.name === newspaper || newspaperInfo.acronym === newspaper)
                ) {
                    return "https://" + newspaperInfo['domain'];
                }
            }
            return 'https://' + nozGlobal.defaultNewspaperConfig.domain;
        },
        getNewspaperInfoByNewspaper: function (newspaper, infoField) {
            if (!infoField) {
                infoField = 'name';
            }
            for (var i = 0; i < nozGlobal.defaultInfos.length; i++) {
                var newspaperInfo = nozGlobal.defaultInfos[i];
                if (newspaperInfo.name === newspaper || newspaperInfo.acronym === newspaper) {
                    return newspaperInfo[infoField];
                }
            }
            return null;
        },
        getLocationByNewspaper: function (newspaper) {
            return this.getNewspaperInfoByNewspaper(newspaper, 'location')
                    ? this.getNewspaperInfoByNewspaper(newspaper, 'location')
                    : nozGlobal.defaultLocation;
        },
        getAcronymByNewspaper: function (newspaper) {
            return this.getNewspaperInfoByNewspaper(newspaper, 'acronym')
                    ? this.getNewspaperInfoByNewspaper(newspaper, 'acronym')
                    : nozGlobal.defaultNewspaperAcronym;
        },
        getNewspaperByLocation: function (location) {
            for (var newspaper in nozGlobal.newspaperLocations) {
                var locations = nozGlobal.newspaperLocations[newspaper];
                for (var i = 0; i < locations.length; i++) {
                    if (locations[i] === location) {
                        return newspaper;
                    }
                }
            }
            return nozGlobal.defaultNewspaper;
        },
        getValueFromGroupAction: function(text) {
            if (typeof c1_headers !== 'undefined') {
                if(c1_headers.hasOwnProperty('C1-Meter-User-Group-Action')) {
                    var c1MeterUserGroupAction = c1_headers['C1-Meter-User-Group-Action'];
                    if(c1MeterUserGroupAction.hasOwnProperty('cms_snippet')) {
                        var c1MeterCmsSnippet = c1MeterUserGroupAction['cms_snippet'];
                        if(c1MeterCmsSnippet.hasOwnProperty('parameters')) {
                            var c1MeterParameters = c1MeterCmsSnippet['parameters'];
                            for(var i = 0; i < c1MeterParameters.length; i++) {
                                var parameters = c1MeterParameters[i];
                                var regexp = new RegExp(text+"(.*)", "g");
                                var match = regexp.exec(parameters);
                                if(match !== null) {
                                    return match[1];
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            } else {
                return 'no c1_headers';
            }
        },
        getValueFromC1Header: function (property) {
            if (typeof c1_headers !== 'undefined') {
                var c1PropertyValue = c1_headers[property];
                if (typeof c1PropertyValue !== 'undefined') {
                    return c1PropertyValue;
                } else {
                    return "property_not_found";
                }
            }
        },
        checkCanonicalTag: function () {
            if (document.querySelector("link[rel='canonical']") !== null) {
                return true;
            } else {
                return false;
            }
        }
    };
  </script>

&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;' data-output-channel-section-id="" data-path-output-channel-section-checkout="https://www.noz.de/personal-news/api/output_channel_section/checkout" data-path-section-add="https://www.noz.de/personal-news/api/sections/add" data-user-id="" href="https://www.noz.de/mehr/meine-nachrichten">

      <aside id="sidenav-holder">
       <div class="sidenav-page" data-page-title="menu">
        <div class="login-button-wrapper">
         <a class="btn btn-primary flat-button login-button btn-block" href="https://www.noz.de/login">
          Anmelden

        <div class="personal-news-button-wrapper">
         <a class="btn btn-primary flat-button btn-block personal-news-button" href="/mehr/meine-nachrichten">
          Meine Nachrichten

        <form action="/suche/" class="sidenav-search" method="GET">

         <script>
          (function () {
                    var userInfos = JSON.parse(userInformation);
                    var flashyAboNote = document.querySelector('.sidenav-flashy-abo-button');
                    if (!flashyAboNote) {
                        return;
                    }
                    if (userInfos.subscription !== undefined && userInfos.subscription && userInfos.subscription.indexOf('digital') === 0) {
                        flashyAboNote.parentNode.removeChild(flashyAboNote);
                    } else {
                        flashyAboNote.classList.remove('hidden');
                    }
                })();
         </script>

        <div class="local-sideNav-choose">
         <div class="sideNav-dropdown-wrapper">
          <input autocapitalize="off" autocomplete="off" autocorrect="off" placeholder="Zeitung | Lokalteil wählen" spellcheck="false" type="text"/>
          <i class="icon-caret-down dropdown-button">

       <div class="sidenav-page" data-ajax-tab-url="/ajax/newspaperSelect?type=sideNav" data-page-title="location-selector">
        <i class="icon-settings icon-spin">
        </i>
       </div>

      <script>
       (function () {
    var header = document.querySelector('.row.header');
    var initialize = function () {
        var setCookie = function () {
            var expireDate = new Date(2099, 1, 1);

            for (var i = 0; i < nozGlobal.defaultInfos.length; i++) {
                var newspaperPath = nozGlobal.defaultInfos[i].parentSlug + nozGlobal.defaultInfos[i].slug,
                    newspaperIsIntern = nozGlobal.defaultInfos[i].isIntern,
                    newspaperDomain = nozGlobal.defaultInfos[i].domain;

                if (window.location.pathname === newspaperPath ||
                    (!newspaperIsIntern && newspaperDomain === window.location.hostname)
                ) {
                    if (cookies.get('selectedNewspaper') !== nozGlobal.defaultInfos[i].name) {
                        cookies.set('selectedNewspaper', encodeURIComponent(nozGlobal.defaultInfos[i].name).replace(/%20/g, '+'), {
                            path: '/',
                            expires: expireDate
                        });
                    }
                    if (!cookies.get('selectedLocation')) {
                        cookies.set('selectedLocation', encodeURIComponent(nozGlobal.defaultInfos[i].location).replace(/%20/g, '+'), {
                            path: '/',
                            expires: expireDate
                        });
                    }
                    break;
                }
            }

            if (!cookies.get('selectedNewspaper') || !cookies.get('selectedLocation') ||
                nozGlobal.defaultNewspaperConfig.domain !== window.location.hostname
            ) {
                var newspaper = nozGlobal.defaultNewspaper;
                // Special case for newspaper articles
                // Set newspaper depending on article newspaper
                var articleNewspaper = document.querySelector('div[itemprop="publisher"] meta[itemprop="name"]');
                if (articleNewspaper) {
                    newspaper = articleNewspaper.getAttribute('content');
                    cookies.set('selectedNewspaper', encodeURIComponent(articleNewspaper).replace(/%20/g, '+'), {
                        path: '/',
                        expires: expireDate
                    });
                }
                cookies.set('selectedNewspaper', encodeURIComponent(newspaper).replace(/%20/g, '+'), {
                    path: '/',
                    expires: expireDate
                });
                cookies.set('selectedLocation', encodeURIComponent(nozGlobal.defaultLocation).replace(/%20/g, '+'), {
                    path: '/',
                    expires: expireDate
                });
            }
        };

        var setLoginButton = function () {
            var userInfos = JSON.parse(userInformation),
                loginButton = header.querySelectorAll('.login-button');

            if (userInfos.redirect) {
                if (window.location.pathname !== '/mehr/nutzerhilfe/mehrfachnutzung') {
                    window.location = userInfos.redirect;
                }
            }

            if (userInfos.name !== "") {
                if (userInfos.name.length > 19) {
                    userInfos.name = userInfos.name.substr(0, 19) + "...";
                }

                if (!cookies.get('loggedin')) {
                    cookies.set('loggedin', 1, {
                        path: '/'
                    });
                }
                var notifications = document.createElement('span');
                if (loginButton.length > 0) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < loginButton.length; i++) {
                        loginButton[i].innerHTML = "<span class='logged-in-button-text'>" + userInfos.name + "</span><i class='icon-user'></i><i class='icon-settings'></i>";
                        loginButton[i].className = loginButton[i].className + ' logged-in-button';
                        loginButton[i].href = '#';
                    }
                }
                if (userInfos.notifications) {
                    var protocol = location.protocol;
                    var url = (protocol == "https:" ? "count_notifications_sec" : "count_notifications"),
                        port = (location.port ? ':' + location.port : '' );
                    nozUtils.sendAjaxRequest('https://' + location.hostname + port + '/' + url + '/' + userInfos.userId, {}, 'get', function (response) {
                        if (parseInt(response, 10) > 0) {
                            notifications.appendChild(document.createTextNode(response));
                            notifications.className = "badge badge-info";
                            for (var i = 0; i < loginButton.length; i++) {
                                loginButton[i].appendChild(notifications);
                            }
                        }
                    }, true);
                }
            } else {
                if (!cookies.get('loggedin') || cookies.get('loggedin') == 1) {
                    cookies.set('loggedin', 0, {
                        path: '/'
                    });
                }
            }
        };
        setCookie();
        if (header) {
            setLoginButton();
        }
    };

    var noCookieMessage = function () {
        var parent = document.getElementById('main-content-without-outside-advertisements'),
            beforeNode = document.getElementById('navigation').nextElementSibling,
            message = document.createElement('DIV');
        message.className = 'row';
        message.innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger" style="cursor: pointer;">' +
            '<button type="button" class="close" data-dismiss="alert">&times;</button>' +
            'Um noz.de in vollem Umfang nutzen zu können, müssen Sie auf Ihrem Computer, Smartphone oder Tablet sogenannte "Cookies" zulassen. Diese Cookies sind standardmäßig aktiviert. Um Ihre Cookies wieder zu aktivieren, klicken Sie bitte hier.';
        parent.insertBefore(message, beforeNode);
        message.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
            if (!nozUtils.hasClass(event.target, 'close')) {
                window.location = "https://www.noz.de/mehr/nutzerhilfe/zulassen_von_cookies";
            }
        })
    };

    window.setTimeout(function () {
        if (navigator.cookieEnabled) {
            initialize();
        } else {
            noCookieMessage();
        }
    }, 0);
})();
      </script>
     </div>
    </div>

    <script>
     (function () {
    var useAnimationFrame = (window.requestAnimationFrame !== undefined && window.cancelAnimationFrame !== undefined),
        navigation = document.querySelector('#navigation'),
        secondLevelNav = (navigation ? navigation.querySelector('.second-level-nav') : null),
        themeLabelHolder = (secondLevelNav ? secondLevelNav.querySelector('.theme-label-holder') : null),
        themeLabels = (themeLabelHolder ? themeLabelHolder.querySelectorAll('.theme-label') : null),
        partialDropDowns = document.querySelectorAll('.partial-drop-down'),
        moreNecessary = false,
        themeTop = false,
        secondLevelExpandetHeight = 0,
        index = 0,
        initAnimationFrame = 0,
        localSelectButton = document.querySelector('#location-select-button'),
        windowWidth = window.innerWidth;

    moveMoreThemes = function (moreThemes) {
        if (moreThemes.getBoundingClientRect().top > themeTop) {
            moreThemes.parentNode.insertBefore(moreThemes, moreThemes.previousSibling);
            moveMoreThemes(moreThemes);

        }
    };

    reFetchElements = function () {
        useAnimationFrame = (window.requestAnimationFrame !== undefined && window.cancelAnimationFrame !== undefined);
        navigation = document.querySelector('#navigation');
        secondLevelNav = (navigation ? navigation.querySelector('.second-level-nav') : null);
        themeLabelHolder = (secondLevelNav ? secondLevelNav.querySelector('.theme-label-holder') : null);
        themeLabels = (themeLabelHolder ? themeLabelHolder.querySelectorAll('.theme-label') : null);
    };

    initThemeLabels = function () {
        var moreThemes = document.querySelector('#theme-label-more');
        if (moreThemes) {
            moreThemes.parentNode.removeChild(moreThemes);
            moreThemes = false;
        }
        themeTop = moreNecessary = false;
        for (index = 0; index < themeLabels.length; index++) {
            if (themeTop === false || themeTop === 0) {
                themeTop = themeLabels[index].getBoundingClientRect().top;
            } else if (themeTop < themeLabels[index].getBoundingClientRect().top) {
                moreNecessary = true;
            }
        }
        if (moreNecessary) {
            moreThemes = document.createElement('a');
            moreThemes.id = 'theme-label-more';
            moreThemes.href = '#';
            moreThemes.innerHTML = 'Mehr <i class="icon-plus"></i>';
            themeLabelHolder.appendChild(moreThemes);
            moreThemes = themeLabelHolder.querySelector('#theme-label-more');
            setTimeout(function () {
                //On mobile we need to delay the execution by a tick to ensure the page is laid out correctly
                //else the more bubble might be out of the viewport
                //seems like the resize event is not properly triggering in that case
                moveMoreThemes(moreThemes);
            }, 0);
            secondLevelExpandetHeight = themeLabelHolder.getBoundingClientRect().height + 10;
            moreThemes.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                if (nozUtils.hasClass(secondLevelNav, 'expanded')) {
                    moreThemes.innerHTML = 'Mehr <i class="icon-plus"></i>';
                    moreThemes.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(187, 187, 187, 1)';
                    secondLevelNav.style.height = '';
                } else {
                    moreThemes.innerHTML = 'Mehr <i class="icon-remove"></i>';
                    moreThemes.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(0, 56, 108, 1)';
                    secondLevelNav.style.height = secondLevelExpandetHeight + 'px';
                }
                nozUtils.toggleClass(secondLevelNav, 'expanded');
                return false;
            });
            moreThemes.addEventListener('mouseenter', function () {
                if (nozUtils.hasClass(secondLevelNav, 'expanded')) {
                    moreThemes.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(187, 187, 187, 1)';
                } else {
                    moreThemes.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(0, 56, 108, 1)';
                }
            });
            moreThemes.addEventListener('mouseleave', function () {
                if (nozUtils.hasClass(secondLevelNav, 'expanded')) {
                    moreThemes.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(0, 56, 108, 1)';
                } else {
                    moreThemes.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(187, 187, 187, 1)';
                }
            });
        }
    };

    if (localSelectButton) {
        function localChooseButtonClickFunc(e) {
            var sideNav = document.querySelector('#sidenav-holder');
            e.preventDefault();
            e.stopPropagation();
            var event = document.createEvent('Event');
            if (!nozUtils.hasClass(sideNav, 'active') || sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-page') !== 'location-selector') {
                sideNav.setAttribute('data-nav-page', 'location-selector');
                event.initEvent('sidenav.open', false, true);
            } else {
                event.initEvent('sidenav.close', false, true);
            }
            sideNav.dispatchEvent(event);

            return false;
        }

        function setHasDefaultLocationCookie() {
            cookies.set('hasDefaultLoc', false, {path: '/'});
        }

         function trackClicks(type) {
            if (typeof MSOdataLayer == "undefined") {
                MSOdataLayer = [];
            }
            MSOdataLayer.push({
                event: 'location-select-button-'+type
            });
        }

        const SELECT_LOC = 'Ort wählen';
        let selectedLoc = SELECT_LOC;

        var userInfo = JSON.parse(userInformation);
        if (userInfo) {
            if (userInfo.userId) {
                if (!userInfo.hasDefaultLocation) {
                    selectedLoc = decodeURIComponent(userInfo.selectedLocation);
                    if (selectedLoc === SELECT_LOC) {
                        selectedLoc = decodeURIComponent(cookies.get('selectedLocation')).replace('+', ' ');
                    }
                } else {
                    localSelectButton.addEventListener('click', localChooseButtonClickFunc);
                    localSelectButton.addEventListener('click', () => {trackClicks('bubble')}, {once: true});
                }
            } else {
                if (cookies.get('hasDefaultLoc') === 'false') {
                    selectedLoc = decodeURIComponent(cookies.get('selectedLocation')).replace('+', ' ');
                } else {
                    localSelectButton.addEventListener('click', localChooseButtonClickFunc);
                    localSelectButton.addEventListener('click', setHasDefaultLocationCookie, {once: true});
                    localSelectButton.addEventListener('click', () => {trackClicks('bubble')}, {once: true});
                }
            }

            if (selectedLoc !== SELECT_LOC) {    const url = '/lokales/' + (nozUtils.replaceUmlaute(selectedLoc).replace(' ', '-').toLowerCase());
                localSelectButton.text = selectedLoc;
                localSelectButton.setAttribute('href', url);
            }

            var icon = document.createElement('i');
            icon.classList.add('icon-settings');
            if (localSelectButton.nextSibling) {
                localSelectButton.after(icon, localSelectButton.nextSibling);
            } else {
                localSelectButton.after(icon);
            }
            icon.addEventListener('click', localChooseButtonClickFunc);
            icon.addEventListener('click', () => {trackClicks('icon')}, {once: true});
        }
    }

    // Set eventListeners for partialDropDowns
    if (partialDropDowns && partialDropDowns.length > 0) {
        var firstEl = document.querySelector('.first-level-nav > a:first-child');
        if (firstEl && firstEl.classList.contains('partial-drop-down')) {
            firstEl.closest('.first-level-nav').style.paddingLeft = 0;
        }

        /**
         * @param node
         */
        var toggleIcon = function (node) {
            if (node instanceof Event) {
                node = node.target;
            }
            var setIcon = 'icon-angle-up';
            var currIcon = node.querySelector('i').classList[0];
            if (currIcon === 'icon-angle-up') {
                setIcon = 'icon-angle-down';
            }

            node.querySelector('i').classList.replace(currIcon, setIcon);
        };

        /**
         * @param event
         * @returns {*}
         */
        var getCorrectDropDownNode = function (event) {
            if (event.target.tagName !== 'A') {
                node = event.target.closest('A');
            } else {
                node = event.target;
            }

            return node;
        };

        /**
         * @param node
         */
        var toggleActive = function (node) {
            node.classList.toggle('active');
        };

        /**
         * @param event
         */
        var showSpinner = function (event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            var node = getCorrectDropDownNode(event);
            if (node.classList.contains('active')) {
                hideSecondLevelNav();
            } else {
                secondLevelNav.style.height = 'auto';
                secondLevelNav.innerHTML = '<i class="icon-spinner icon-spin"></i>';
            }

            toggleIcon(node);
            toggleActive(node);
        };

        /**
         * @param event
         */
        var showContent = function (event) {
            event.preventDefault ? event.preventDefault() : (event.returnValue = false);

            node = getCorrectDropDownNode(event);
            var toggle = secondLevelNav.innerHTML !== '<i class="icon-spinner icon-spin"></i>';
            if (node.classList.contains('active') && toggle) {
                hideSecondLevelNav(node);
            } else {
                secondLevelNav.style.height = 'auto';
                var content = node.dataset.snc;
                var re = /(<a href=.*?>(.*?_HIDDEN_DESKTOP)<\/a>)/g;
                while ((found = re.exec(content)) !== null) {
                    var newLink = document.createElement('a');
                    newLink.text = found[2].replace('_HIDDEN_DESKTOP', '');
                    newLink.classList.add('hidden-desktop');
                    content = content.replace(found[1], newLink.outerHTML);
                }
                secondLevelNav.innerHTML = content;
                secondLevelNav.querySelector('i.icon-remove').addEventListener('click', function (event) {
                    var node = document.querySelector('.first-level-nav .active');
                    hideSecondLevelNav();
                    toggleActive(node);
                    toggleIcon(node);
                });
            }

            if (toggle) {
                toggleIcon(node);
                toggleActive(node);
            }
        };

        var hideSecondLevelNav = function () {
            secondLevelNav.innerHTML = navigation.dataset.secondLevelOrig;
            secondLevelNav.style.height = '50px';
            reFetchElements();
            initThemeLabels();
        };

        // Store the initial second level navigation
        if (partialDropDowns.length > 0) {
            navigation.dataset.secondLevelOrig = secondLevelNav.innerHTML;
        }

        if (window.NodeList && !NodeList.prototype.forEach) {
            NodeList.prototype.forEach = Array.prototype.forEach;
        }

        partialDropDowns.forEach(function (dropDown) {
            var secondLevelNav = document.querySelector('.second-level-nav'),
                url = dropDown.dataset.contentUrl;
            if (url !== '') {
                var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest(),
                    method = "GET",
                    url = url;
                xhr.open(method, url, true);
                xhr.onreadystatechange = function () {
                    if (xhr.readyState === 4 && xhr.status === 200) {
                        dropDown.dataset.snc = xhr.response;
                        dropDown.removeEventListener('click', showSpinner);
                        dropDown.addEventListener('click', showContent);
                        if (secondLevelNav.innerHTML === '<i class="icon-spinner icon-spin"></i>') {
                            dropDown.click();
                        }
                    }
                };
                xhr.send();
            }

            dropDown.addEventListener('click', showSpinner);
        });
    }

    if (themeLabels && themeLabels.length > 0) {
        for (index = 0; index < themeLabels.length; index++) {
            themeLabels[index].addEventListener('mouseenter', function (e) {
                e.target.style.backgroundColor = e.target.getAttribute('data-hover-color');
            });
            themeLabels[index].addEventListener('mouseleave', function (e) {
                e.target.style.backgroundColor = '';
            });
        }
        initThemeLabels();
        window.addEventListener('resize', function () {
            if (windowWidth !== window.innerWidth) {
                windowWidth = window.innerWidth;
                if (useAnimationFrame) {
                    window.cancelAnimationFrame(initAnimationFrame);
                    initAnimationFrame = window.requestAnimationFrame(function () {
                        initThemeLabels();
                    });
                } else {
                    window.clearTimeout(initAnimationFrame);
                    initAnimationFrame = window.setTimeout(function () {
                        initThemeLabels();
                    }, 100);
                }
            }
        });
    } else {
        if (secondLevelNav) {
            var ua = window.navigator.userAgent;
            if (ua.indexOf('MSIE') === -1 || ua.indexOf('Trident') === -1 || ua.indexOf('Edge') === -1) {
                secondLevelNav.removeChild(secondLevelNav.querySelector(':scope>span'));
            }
        }
    }
})();
    </script>
    <!-- Side nav -->
    <script>
     (function () {
    var header = document.querySelector('.row.header'),
        sideNav = document.querySelector('#sidenav-holder'),
        useAnimationFrame = (window.requestAnimationFrame !== undefined && window.cancelAnimationFrame !== undefined),
        animationFrame = 0,
        oldHeight = 0,
        checkSize = function () {
            var headerRect = header.getBoundingClientRect(),
                newHeight = window.innerHeight - headerRect.height + 5;
            if (oldHeight !== newHeight) {
                sideNav.style.maxHeight = newHeight + 'px';
                oldHeight = newHeight;
            }
        },
        sideNavResize = function (timeout) {
            if (useAnimationFrame) {
                window.cancelAnimationFrame(animationFrame);
                animationFrame = window.requestAnimationFrame(checkSize);
            } else {
                window.clearTimeout(animationFrame);
                animationFrame = window.setTimeout(checkSize, timeout);
            }
        },
        queueScroll = function () {
            sideNavResize(500);
        },
        queueResize = function () {
            sideNavResize(100);
        };
    if (header && sideNav) {
        var menuBtn = header.querySelector('.header-menu button'),
            searchButton = header.querySelector('.header-search i'),
            loginButton = header.querySelector('.right-header .login-button'),
            localChooseButton = header.querySelector('.header-local-choose'),
            sideNavLoginButton = sideNav.querySelector('.login-button'),
            searchField = sideNav.querySelector('.sidenav-search'),
            localChoose = sideNav.querySelector('.sideNav-dropdown-wrapper'),
            pages = sideNav.querySelectorAll('.sidenav-page'),
            formSigninButton = sideNav.querySelector('.form-signin button[type="submit"]');

        window.addEventListener('resize', queueResize);
        window.addEventListener('scroll', queueScroll);
        sideNavResize(10);

        //get NavPages
        var navPages = document.querySelectorAll('#sidenav-pages-holder .sidenav-page'),
            menuFirstLevelNav = document.querySelector('#sidenav-pages-holder .menu-nav-holder');
        if (navPages.length > 0) {
            if (menuFirstLevelNav) {
                if (searchField) {
                    searchField.parentNode.insertBefore(menuFirstLevelNav, searchField.nextElementSibling);
                }
            }
            pages = sideNav.querySelectorAll('.sidenav-page');
        }

        //set NavLinkHandler
        var navLinks = sideNav.querySelectorAll('.sidenav-nav-page-link'),
            navBackLinks = sideNav.querySelectorAll('.sidenav-nav-page-back-link'),
            navLinkClickFunc = function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                var nodeId = (e.target.tagName.toUpperCase() == 'I' ? e.target.parentNode.getAttribute('data-node-id') : e.target.getAttribute('data-node-id'));
                if (nodeId) {
                    var event = document.createEvent('Event');
                    event.initEvent('sidenav.open', false, true);
                    if (parseInt(nodeId, 10) === 1) {
                        sideNav.setAttribute('data-nav-page', 'menu');
                        sideNav.removeAttribute('data-nav-node-id');
                    } else {
                        sideNav.setAttribute('data-nav-page', 'nav-page');
                        sideNav.setAttribute('data-nav-node-id', nodeId);
                    }
                    sideNav.dispatchEvent(event);
                }
                return false;
            },
            navBackLinkClickFunc = function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                if (sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-page') == 'nav-page' && sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-node-id')) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < pages.length; i++) {
                        if ('nav-page' == pages[i].getAttribute('data-page-title')
                            && sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-node-id') == pages[i].getAttribute('data-node-id')) {
                            nozUtils.removeClass(pages[i], 'active');
                        }
                    }
                }
                navLinkClickFunc(e);
                return false;
            };
        for (var i = 0; i < navLinks.length; i++) {
            navLinks[i].addEventListener('click', navLinkClickFunc);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < navBackLinks.length; i++) {
            navBackLinks[i].addEventListener('click', navBackLinkClickFunc);
        }

        sideNav.addEventListener('sidenav.open', function (e) {
            if (sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-page') && pages.length > 0) {
                var navPageFound = false;
                for (var i = 0; i < pages.length; i++) {
                    if (menuBtn) {
                        nozUtils.setClass(menuBtn, 'open');
                    }
                    switch (sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-page')) {
                        case 'nav-page':
                            if (pages[i].getAttribute('data-page-title') === sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-page')
                                && pages[i].getAttribute('data-node-id') === sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-node-id')) {
                                nozUtils.setClass(pages[i], 'active');
                                navPageFound = true;
                            } else if (pages[i].getAttribute('data-page-title') !== sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-page')) {
                                nozUtils.removeClass(pages[i], 'active');
                            }
                            break;
                        default:
                            if (pages[i].getAttribute('data-page-title') === sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-page')) {
                                nozUtils.setClass(pages[i], 'active');
                                navPageFound = true;
                            } else {
                                nozUtils.removeClass(pages[i], 'active');
                            }
                    }
                    if (pages[i].getAttribute('data-ajax-tab-url')) {
                        nozUtils.ajaxElemContentLoad(pages[i].getAttribute('data-ajax-tab-url'), pages[i], function (elem) {
                            var backButton = elem.querySelector('.sidenav-nav-page-back-link');
                            if (backButton) {
                                backButton.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                                    var nodeId = e.target.getAttribute('data-node-id'),
                                        sideNav = document.querySelector('#sidenav-holder');
                                    if (sideNav && nodeId) {
                                        e.preventDefault();
                                        var event = document.createEvent('Event');
                                        event.initEvent('sidenav.open', false, true);
                                        if (parseInt(nodeId, 10) === 1) {
                                            sideNav.setAttribute('data-nav-page', 'menu');
                                            sideNav.removeAttribute('data-nav-node-id');
                                        } else {
                                            sideNav.setAttribute('data-nav-page', 'nav-page');
                                            sideNav.setAttribute('data-nav-node-id', nodeId);
                                        }
                                        sideNav.dispatchEvent(event);
                                        return false;
                                    }
                                });
                            }
                            var newspaperSelect = elem.querySelector('.newspaper-select');
                            if (newspaperSelect) {
                                var event = document.createEvent('Event');
                                event.initEvent('sideNavLocationSelectLoaded', false, true);
                                sideNav.dispatchEvent(event);
                                nozUtils.setClass(sideNav, 'sideNav-location-select-loaded');
                            }
                        });
                        pages[i].removeAttribute('data-ajax-tab-url');
                    }
                }
                nozUtils.setClass(sideNav, 'active');

                if (!navPageFound) {
                    if (sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-page') === 'nav-page') {
                        for (var i = 0; i < navPages.length; i++) {
                            var nodeId = navPages[i].getAttribute('data-node-id');
                            if (nodeId === sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-node-id')) {
                                navPages[i].querySelectorAll('a').forEach(function(e){
                                    if (e.text.indexOf('_HIDDEN_DESKTOP') !== -1) {
                                        e.innerHTML = e.innerHTML.replace('_HIDDEN_DESKTOP', '')
                                    }
                                });
                                sideNav.appendChild(navPages[i]);
                                navPageFound = true;
                                pages = sideNav.querySelectorAll('.sidenav-page');
                                navPages = document.querySelectorAll('#sidenav-pages-holder .sidenav-page');
                                var newPage = sideNav.querySelector('.sidenav-page[data-node-id="' + nodeId + '"]');
                                var navLinksNewPage = newPage.querySelectorAll('.sidenav-nav-page-link'),
                                    navBackLinksNewPage = newPage.querySelectorAll('.sidenav-nav-page-back-link');
                                for (var j = 0; j < navLinksNewPage.length; j++) {
                                    navLinksNewPage[j].addEventListener('click', navLinkClickFunc);
                                }
                                for (var j = 0; j < navBackLinksNewPage.length; j++) {
                                    navBackLinksNewPage[j].addEventListener('click', navBackLinkClickFunc);
                                }
                                //notwendig um den Slideeffekt zu erhalten
                                var activateFunc = function (pg) {
                                    window.setTimeout(function () {
                                        nozUtils.setClass(pg, 'active');
                                    }, 100);
                                };
                                activateFunc(newPage);
                                break;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                if (!navPageFound) {
                    var event = document.createEvent('Event');
                    event.initEvent('sidenav.close', false, true);
                    sideNav.dispatchEvent(event);
                }
            }

            document.querySelector('body').addEventListener('click', function close (e) {
                if ($(e.target).parents('#sidenav-holder').length <= 0 && e.target.id !== 'sidenav-holder'
                    && !e.target.classList.contains('header-search')
                    && !e.target.classList.contains('icon-search')
                ) {
                    var event = document.createEvent('Event');
                    event.initEvent('sidenav.close', false, true);
                    sideNav.dispatchEvent(event);
                    document.querySelector('body').removeEventListener('click', 'close', false);
                }
            });
        });
        sideNav.addEventListener('sidenav.close', function (e) {
            sideNav.removeAttribute('data-nav-page');
            sideNav.removeAttribute('data-nav-node-id');
            if (menuBtn) {
                nozUtils.removeClass(menuBtn, 'open');
            }
            nozUtils.removeClass(sideNav, 'active');
            for (var i = 0; i < pages.length; i++) {
                nozUtils.removeClass(pages[i], 'active');
            }
        });

        //Handle Buttons
        if (menuBtn) {
            menuBtn.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                var event = document.createEvent('Event');
                if (!nozUtils.hasClass(sideNav, 'active')) {
                    sideNav.setAttribute('data-nav-page', 'menu');
                    event.initEvent('sidenav.open', false, true);
                } else {
                    event.initEvent('sidenav.close', false, true);
                }
                sideNav.dispatchEvent(event);

                e.stopPropagation();
            }, true);
        }
        if (searchButton) {
            searchButton.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                if (searchField) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    var event = document.createEvent('Event');
                    var searchInput = searchField.querySelector('input');
                    if (!nozUtils.hasClass(sideNav, 'active') || sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-page') !== 'menu') {
                        sideNav.setAttribute('data-nav-page', 'menu');
                        event.initEvent('sidenav.open', false, true);
                        if (searchInput) {
                            searchInput.focus();
                        }
                    } else {
                        if (document.activeElement !== searchInput) {
                            searchInput.focus();
                            event.initEvent('sidenav.open', false, true);
                        } else {
                            event.initEvent('sidenav.close', false, true);
                        }
                    }
                    sideNav.dispatchEvent(event);
                    return false;
                }
                e.stopPropagation();
            }, true);
        }
        if (loginButton) {
            loginButton.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                var event = document.createEvent('Event');
                if (!nozUtils.hasClass(sideNav, 'active') || sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-page') !== 'user-menu') {
                    sideNav.setAttribute('data-nav-page', 'user-menu');
                    event.initEvent('sidenav.open', false, true);
                } else {
                    event.initEvent('sidenav.close', false, true);
                }
                sideNav.dispatchEvent(event);
                e.stopPropagation();

                return false;
            }, true);
        }
        if (sideNavLoginButton) {
            sideNavLoginButton.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                var event = document.createEvent('Event');
                if (!nozUtils.hasClass(sideNav, 'active') || sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-page') !== 'user-menu') {
                    sideNav.setAttribute('data-nav-page', 'user-menu');
                    event.initEvent('sidenav.open', false, true);
                } else {
                    event.initEvent('sidenav.close', false, true);
                }
                sideNav.dispatchEvent(event);
                e.stopPropagation();

                return false;
            }, true);
        }
        if (localChoose) {
            var localChooseClickFunc = function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                localChoose.querySelector('input').blur();
                var event = document.createEvent('Event');
                sideNav.setAttribute('data-nav-page', 'location-selector');
                event.initEvent('sidenav.open', false, true);
                sideNav.dispatchEvent(event);
                return false;
            };
            localChoose.addEventListener('click', localChooseClickFunc);
            localChoose.querySelector('input').addEventListener('click', localChooseClickFunc);
            localChoose.querySelector('.dropdown-button').addEventListener('click', localChooseClickFunc);
            if (undefined == cookies.get('usePredefined') || 'true' == cookies.get('usePredefined')) {
                localChoose.querySelector('input').value = "Zeitung | Lokalteil wählen";
            } else if (cookies.get('selectedLocation')) {
                localChoose.querySelector('input').value = decodeURIComponent(cookies.get('selectedLocation').replace(/\+/, '%20'));
            } else {
                localChoose.querySelector('input').value = nozGlobal.defaultLocation;
            }
        }
        if (localChooseButton) {
            var localChooseButtonClickFunc = function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
                var event = document.createEvent('Event');
                if (!nozUtils.hasClass(sideNav, 'active') || sideNav.getAttribute('data-nav-page') !== 'location-selector') {
                    sideNav.setAttribute('data-nav-page', 'location-selector');
                    event.initEvent('sidenav.open', false, true);
                } else {
                    event.initEvent('sidenav.close', false, true);
                }
                sideNav.dispatchEvent(event);
                return false;
            };
            localChooseButton.addEventListener('click', localChooseButtonClickFunc);

            if (undefined == cookies.get('usePredefined') || 'true' == cookies.get('usePredefined')) {
                localChooseButton.querySelector('i').setAttribute('data-content', "Zeitung | Lokalteil wählen");
            } else if (cookies.get('selectedLocation')) {
                localChooseButton.querySelector('i').setAttribute('data-content', decodeURIComponent(cookies.get('selectedLocation').replace(/\+/, '%20')));
            } else {
                localChooseButton.querySelector('i').setAttribute('data-content', nozGlobal.defaultLocation);
            }
        }
    }
})();
    </script>

         <script>
          $(function () {
    $('.list-img-wrapper-bg').filter(function () {
        return $(this)[0].style.backgroundColor != "";
    }).children('img').on('load', function() {
        $(this).closest('.list-img-wrapper-bg').one('mouseenter mouseleave', function() {
            $(this)[0].style.backgroundColor = "";
        });
    });
    $(window).on('load nozLoad', function() {
        $('.list-img-wrapper-bg').filter(function () {
            return $(this)[0].style.backgroundColor != "";
        }).children('img').on('load', function() {
            $(this).closest('.list-img-wrapper-bg').one('mouseenter mouseleave', function() {
                $(this)[0].style.backgroundColor = "";
            });
        });
    });
    //Native Ad
    $('body').on('nativeAdEmpty', function (e) {
        var target = $(e.target),
            row = target.closest('.row');
        if(target.closest('.article-list-first-big').length > 0) {
            if(row.find('.span6:not([style*="display: none"])').length % 2 != 1) {
                row.find('article.hidden').first().removeClass('hidden').parent().css('display', 'inherit')
            }
            target.parent().remove();
            $(window).trigger('nozLoad')
        }
    });
    $('.edit-buttons a.delete').on('click', function () {
        return confirm('Soll der Eintrag wirklich gelöscht werden?');
    });
});
         </script>

       <div class="row-fluid row-break-mobile">
        <div class="span4">
         <article class="small-article" data-id="2263036">
          <div class="list-img-icon-wrapper">

        (function () {
            function appendPersonalizationElement(prototypeElement, recommendedItem, isCeleraOneBox) {
                var personalizationElement = nozUtils.htmlToElement(prototypeElement.dataset.prototype, null).childNodes[0],
                    overlineLink = personalizationElement.querySelector('.img-title a'),
                    headlineLink = personalizationElement.querySelector('a.article-link'),
                    imageLink = personalizationElement.querySelector('a.list-img-wrapper'),
                    image = personalizationElement.querySelector('img'),
                    linkUrl = recommendedItem.link_url;
                overlineLink.setAttribute('href', linkUrl);
                overlineLink.innerHTML = recommendedItem.kicker;
                headlineLink.setAttribute('href', linkUrl);
                headlineLink.innerHTML = recommendedItem.title;
                imageLink.setAttribute('href', linkUrl);
                image.setAttribute('src', recommendedItem.teaser_image_url);
                prototypeElement.appendChild(personalizationElement);

                if (isCeleraOneBox) {
                    $(personalizationElement).on('click', function () {
                        if (typeof MSOdataLayer == "undefined") {
                            MSOdataLayer = [];
                        }
                        MSOdataLayer.push({
                            "event": "c1TeaserClick"
                        });
                    })
                }

            }

            function personalization(data) {
                if (typeof (data.content_recommendations) !== "undefined" &&
                    typeof (data.content_recommendations.recommended_items) !== "undefined"
                ) {
                    var recommendedItems = data.content_recommendations.recommended_items;
                    if (recommendedItems.length && recommendedItems.length > 0) {
                        var personalizationBox = document.getElementById('c1-personalization'),
                            mostReadBoxes = document.getElementsByClassName('most-read-personalization'),
                            mostReadBox = mostReadBoxes.length > 0 ? mostReadBoxes[0] : null,
                            userInfos = JSON.parse(userInformation);
                        if (personalizationBox) {
                            for (var i = 0; i < recommendedItems.length && i < 1; i++) {
                                appendPersonalizationElement(personalizationBox, recommendedItems[i], true);
                            }
                        }
                        if (mostReadBox && userInfos.userId) {
                            if (!disableC1ContentPersonalization) {
                                mostReadBox.innerHTML = '';
                                mostReadBox.className = mostReadBox.className + ' content-c1';
                                for (var i = 0; i < recommendedItems.length && i < 3; i++) {
                                    appendPersonalizationElement(mostReadBox, recommendedItems[i], false);
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            function userStatus(response) {
                if (response.data) {
                    c1Response = response.data;

                    try {
                          if (typeof (cre_templateclient) !== "undefined") {
                              cre_templateclient.show({"tracking_response": response.data});
                          }
                          personalization(response.data);
                    } catch (e) {
                        console.log(e);
                    }

                    // notify listeners
                    document.body.dataset.paywallStatus = 'ready';
                    var event = document.createEvent('Event');
                    event.initEvent('paywallStatusReady', true, true);
                    document.body.dispatchEvent(event);

                    // notify personal news recommendation box
                    document.createEvent('Event');
                    event.initEvent('PersonalNews', true, true);
                    document.body.dispatchEvent(event);
                }
            }

            function trackingCall() {
                if (typeof (cre_client) !== "undefined") {
                    var navInfo = $('#navigation'),
                        breadcrumb = navInfo.data('breadcrumb');

                    if (navInfo.length > 0) {
                        if (window.location.pathname.match(/^\/suche/)) {
                            cre_client.set_channel("9999");
                        } else if (breadcrumb) {
                            cre_client.set_channel(breadcrumb);
                        }
                    }

                    cre_client.set_origin("web");
                    cre_client.set_service_id("noz");

                    var selectedNewspaper = decodeURIComponent(cookies.get('selectedNewspaper').replace(/\+/g, '%20'));

                    if (selectedNewspaper === 'Delmenhorster Kreisblatt') {
                        cre_client.set_site("www.dk-online.de");
                    } else {
                        cre_client.set_site("www.noz.de");
                    }

                    cre_client.set_content_id(window.location.pathname);
                    cre_client.set_cms_id("15");
                    cre_client.set_doc_type("homepage");
                    cre_client.set_heading("NOZ – Aktuelle Nachrichten, Bilder und Videos aus der Region Osnabrück, Emsland, Delmenhorst - Neuen Osnabrücker Zeitung | noz.de");
                                                                                                    cre_client.addListener(userStatus);
                                        cre_client.request();
                } else {
                    setTimeout(trackingCall, 1000);
                }
            }

            var trackingBuyCall = function () {
                if (typeof (cre_client) !== "undefined") {
                    // Send by call when confirm page was submitted.
                    // Content id is the path of the url without the .../confirm/xxx.
                    // Example: https://www.noz.de/abo/order/digital_premium/confirm/xxx => /abo/order/digital_premium
                    var uriparts = location.pathname.split('/');
                    var contentId = uriparts.slice(0, -2).join('/');

                    cre_client.set_content_id(contentId);
                    cre_client.request();
                }
            };

            trackingCall();

            $('.abo-form.abo-form-confirm').submit(trackingBuyCall);
        })();

                    // expandable = document.querySelector('#nozmhn_inread iframe');

                    // var logo = header.querySelector('img.logo');
                    // var nozMediaLogo = document.createElement('img');
                    // nozMediaLogo.id = 'noz-media-logo';
                    // nozMediaLogo.className = 'no-hover';
                    // nozMediaLogo.src = logo.dataset.nozMediaSrc;
                    // logo.insertAdjacentHTML('afterend', nozMediaLogo.outerHTML);

                    var stickyHeader = function() {
                        if (header) {
                            var expandable = document.querySelector('#nozmhn_active_expandable_ad_1 iframe');
                            if (expandable) {
                                var expandableTop = expandable.getBoundingClientRect().top + 'px';
                            }
                            var lastScrolledPosition = 0;

                            var stickyHeaderFunc = function() {
                                var scrollTop = -(document.querySelector('html').getBoundingClientRect().top);

                                if (checkWindowWidth(767)) {
                                    nozUtils.removeClass(header, 'sticky');
                                    body.style.paddingTop = 0;
                                } else {
                                    if (scrollTop > lastScrolledPosition) {
                                        //console.log('DOWN');
                                        lastScrolledPosition = scrollTop;
                                        if (scrollTop > headerHeight) {
                                            nozUtils.setClass(header, 'slide-top');
                                            if (typeof expandable !== "undefined" && expandable !== null) {
                                                expandable.style.top = "0px";
                                                if (scrollTop >= window.screen.height * 1.5) {
                                                    expandable.style.position = "sticky";
                                                }
                                            }
                                        }
                                    } else if (scrollTop < lastScrolledPosition) {
                                        //console.log('UP');
                                        lastScrolledPosition = scrollTop;
                                        nozUtils.removeClass(header, 'slide-top');
                                        if (typeof expandable !== "undefined" && expandable !== null) {
                                            expandable.style.top = expandableTop;
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            };

                            window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
                                if (useAnimationFrame) {
                                    window.cancelAnimationFrame(scrollAnimationFrame);
                                    scrollAnimationFrame = window.requestAnimationFrame(stickyHeaderFunc);
                                } else {
                                    window.clearTimeout(scrollAnimationFrame);
                                    scrollAnimationFrame = window.setTimeout(stickyHeaderFunc, 50);
                                }
                            });

                            window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
                                if (useAnimationFrame) {
                                    window.cancelAnimationFrame(scrollAnimationFrame);
                                    scrollAnimationFrame = window.requestAnimationFrame(stickyHeaderFunc);
                                } else {
                                    window.clearTimeout(scrollAnimationFrame);
                                    scrollAnimationFrame = window.setTimeout(stickyHeaderFunc, 50);
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    };

                    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
                        body.style.paddingTop = headerHeight + 'px';
                        nozUtils.setClass(header, 'sticky');
                        stickyHeader();
                    });

                    return stickyHeader;
                })();
            }
  </script>
  <!-- /stickyHeader End -->
  <!-- Webpush -->
  <!-- / Webpush -->
  <script>
   $(function () {
    var userInfos = JSON.parse(userInformation);
    var layers = false;
    if(userInfos){
        layers = userInfos.layers;
    }
    if (layers) {
        layers = JSON.parse(layers);
        for (var capping in layers){
            for(var layer in layers[capping]) {
                var shown = cookies.get('ml_'+capping+'_'+layers[capping][layer]);
                if (shown != undefined && shown !== '') {
                    layers[capping].splice(layer, 1);
                }
                if (layers[capping].length == 0) {
                    delete layers[capping];
                }
            }
        }
        if (Object.keys(layers).length > 0){
            // layerSplit = layers[0].split('_');
            layers = layers[Object.keys(layers)[0]];
            layer = layers.shift();
            $.ajax({
                url: '/marketing_layer/'+layer
            }).done(function(result){
                if (result != '') {
                    $('body').append('<div class="overlayForm"></div>').append(result.layerHtml);
                    var date = new Date();
                    switch (parseInt(capping)) {
                        case 1:
                            date.setDate(date.getDate()+parseInt(capping));
                            break;
                        case 2:
                            date.setMonth(date.getMonth()+1);
                    }
                    cookies.set('ml_'+capping+'_'+layer, true, {
                        expires: date,
                        path: '/'
                    });

                    $('#marketing_layer div.close-button').on('click', function(){
                        $(this).parents('#marketing_layer').remove();
                        $('.overlayForm').remove();
                    })
                }
            });
        }
    }
});
  </script>
  <script>
   /*!
 * ATTENTION this plugin was modified by NOZ-Digital see bug request [NOZ-12205]
 * PR is submitted https://github.com/jasny/jquery.smartbanner/pull/102
 *
 *
 * jQuery Smart Banner
 * Copyright (c) 2012 Arnold Daniels <arnold@jasny.net>
 * Based on 'jQuery Smart Web App Banner' by Kurt Zenisek @ kzeni.com
 */
(function(root, factory) {
  if (typeof define == 'function' && define.amd) {
    define(['jquery'], factory);
  } else {
    factory(root.jQuery);
  }
})(this, function($) {
  var UA = navigator.userAgent;
  var isEdge = /Edge/i.test(UA);

  var SmartBanner = function(options) {
    // Get the original margin-top of the HTML element so we can take that into account.
    this.origHtmlMargin = parseFloat($('html').css('margin-top'));
    this.options = $.extend({}, $.smartbanner.defaults, options);

    // Check if it's already a standalone web app or running within a webui view of an app (not mobile safari).
    var standalone = navigator.standalone;

    // Detect banner type (iOS or Android).
    if (this.options.force) {
      this.type = this.options.force;
    }
    else if (UA.match(/Windows Phone/i) !== null && UA.match(/Edge|Touch/i) !== null) {
      this.type = 'windows';
    }
    else if (UA.match(/iPhone|iPod/i) !== null || (UA.match(/iPad/) && this.options.iOSUniversalApp)) {
      if (UA.match(/Safari/i) !== null &&
          (UA.match(/CriOS/i) !== null ||
           UA.match(/FxiOS/i) != null ||
            window.Number(UA.substr(UA.indexOf('OS ') + 3, 3).replace('_', '.')) < 6)) {
        // Check webview and native smart banner support (iOS 6+).
        this.type = 'ios';
      }
    }
    else if (UA.match(/\bSilk\/(.*\bMobile Safari\b)?/) || UA.match(/\bKF\w/) || UA.match('Kindle Fire')) {
      this.type = 'kindle';
    }
    else if (UA.match(/Android/i) !== null) {
      this.type = 'android';
    }
    // Don't show banner if device isn't iOS or Android, website is loaded in app or user dismissed banner.
    if (!this.type || standalone || this.getCookie('sb-closed') || this.getCookie('sb-installed')) {
      return;
    }
    // Calculate scale.
    this.scale = this.options.scale == 'auto' ? $(window).width() / window.screen.width : this.options.scale;
    if (this.scale < 1) {
      this.scale = 1;
    }
    // Get info from meta data.
    var meta = $(
      this.type == 'android'
        ? 'meta[name="google-play-app"]'
        : (this.type == 'ios'
            ? 'meta[name="apple-itunes-app"]'
            : (this.type == 'kindle'
                ? 'meta[name="kindle-fire-app"]'
                : 'meta[name="msApplication-ID"]'
              )
          )
    );

    if (!meta.length) {
      return;
    }
    // For Windows Store apps, get the PackageFamilyName for protocol launch.
    if (this.type == 'windows') {
      if (isEdge) {
        this.appId = $('meta[name="msApplication-PackageEdgeName"]').attr('content');
      }
      if (!this.appId) {
        this.appId = $('meta[name="msApplication-PackageFamilyName"]').attr('content');
      }
    }
    else {
      // Try to pull the appId out of the meta tag and store the result.
      var parsedMetaContent = /app-id=([^\s,]+)/.exec(meta.attr('content'));
      if (parsedMetaContent) {
        this.appId = parsedMetaContent[1];
      } else {
        return;
      }
    }
    this.title = this.options.title
      ? this.options.title
      : (meta.data('title') || $('title').text().replace(/\s*[|\-·].*$/, ''));

    this.author = this.options.author
      ? this.options.author
      : (meta.data('author') || ($('meta[name="author"]').length ? $('meta[name="author"]').attr('content') : window.location.hostname));

    this.iconUrl = meta.data('iconUrl');
    this.price = meta.data('price');

    // Set default onInstall callback if not set in options.
    if (typeof this.options.onInstall == 'function') {
      this.options.onInstall = this.options.onInstall;
    } else {
      this.options.onInstall = function() {};
    }
    // Set default onClose callback if not set in options.
    if (typeof this.options.onClose == 'function') {
      this.options.onClose = this.options.onClose;
    } else {
      this.options.onClose = function() {};
    }
    // Create banner.
    this.create();
    this.show();
    this.listen();
  };

  ////////////////////////////////////////////
  // NOZ-Digital - change function position //
  ////////////////////////////////////////////
  $.fn.emulateTransitionEnd = function(duration) {
      var called = false, $el = this;
      $(this).one($.support.transition.end, function() {
          called = true;
      });
      var callback = function() {
          if (!called) {
              $($el).trigger($.support.transition.end);
          }
      };
      setTimeout(callback, duration);
      return this;
  };

  SmartBanner.prototype = {

    constructor: SmartBanner,

    create: function() {
      var iconURL;
      var price = this.price || this.options.price;

      var link = this.options.url || (function() {
        switch (this.type) {
          case 'android':
            return 'market://details?id=';
          case 'kindle':
            return 'amzn://apps/android?asin=';
          case 'windows':
            return isEdge
              ? 'ms-windows-store://pdp/?productid='
              : 'ms-windows-store:navigate?appid=';
        }
        return 'https://itunes.apple.com/' + this.options.appStoreLanguage + '/app/id';
      }.call(this) + this.appId);

      var inStore = !price ? '' : (function() {
        var result = price + ' - ';
        switch (this.type) {
          case 'android':
            return result + this.options.inGooglePlay;
          case 'kindle':
            return result + this.options.inAmazonAppStore;
          case 'windows':
            return result + this.options.inWindowsStore;
        }
        return result + this.options.inAppStore
      }.call(this));

      var gloss = this.options.iconGloss == null
        ? (this.type=='ios')
        : this.options.iconGloss;

      if (this.type == 'android' && this.options.GooglePlayParams) {
        link += '&referrer=' + this.options.GooglePlayParams;
      }
      var banner = (
        '<div id="smartbanner" class="' + this.type + '">' +
          '<div class="sb-container">' +
            '<a href="#" class="sb-close">&times;</a>' +
            '<span class="sb-icon"></span>' +
            '<div class="sb-info">' +
              '<strong>' + this.title + '</strong>' +
              '<span>' + this.author + '</span>' +
              '<span>' + inStore + '</span>' +
            '</div>' +
            '<a href="' + link + '" class="sb-button">' +
              '<span>' + this.options.button + '</span>' +
            '</a>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>'
      );
      if (this.options.layer) {
        $(this.options.appendToSelector).append(banner);
      } else {
        $(this.options.appendToSelector).prepend(banner);
      }
      if (this.options.icon) {
        iconURL = this.options.icon;
      } else if(this.iconUrl) {
        iconURL = this.iconUrl;
      } else if ($('link[rel="apple-touch-icon-precomposed"]').length > 0) {
        iconURL = $('link[rel="apple-touch-icon-precomposed"]').attr('href');
        if (this.options.iconGloss == null) {
          gloss = false;
        }
      } else if ($('link[rel="apple-touch-icon"]').length > 0) {
        iconURL = $('link[rel="apple-touch-icon"]').attr('href');
      } else if ($('meta[name="msApplication-TileImage"]').length > 0) {
        iconURL = $('meta[name="msApplication-TileImage"]').attr('content');
      } else if ($('meta[name="msapplication-TileImage"]').length > 0) {
        // Redundant because ms docs show two case usages.
        iconURL = $('meta[name="msapplication-TileImage"]').attr('content');
      }
      if (iconURL) {
        $('#smartbanner .sb-icon').css('background-image', 'url(' + iconURL + ')');
        if (gloss) {
          $('#smartbanner .sb-icon').addClass('gloss');
        }
      } else{
        $('#smartbanner').addClass('no-icon');
      }
      this.bannerHeight = $('#smartbanner').outerHeight() + 2;

      if (this.scale > 1) {
        $('#smartbanner')
          .css('top', parseFloat($('#smartbanner').css('top')) * this.scale)
          .css('height', parseFloat($('#smartbanner').css('height')) * this.scale)
          .hide();
        $('#smartbanner .sb-container')
          .css('-webkit-transform', 'scale(' + this.scale + ')')
          .css('-msie-transform', 'scale(' + this.scale + ')')
          .css('-moz-transform', 'scale(' + this.scale + ')')
          .css('width', $(window).width() / this.scale);
      }
      $('#smartbanner')
        .css('position', this.options.layer ? 'absolute' : 'static');
    },

    listen: function() {
      $('#smartbanner .sb-close').on('click', $.proxy(this.close, this));
      $('#smartbanner .sb-button').on('click', $.proxy(this.install, this));
    },

    show: function(callback) {
      var banner = $('#smartbanner');
      banner.stop();

      if (this.options.layer) {
        banner
          .animate({ top: 0, display: 'block' }, this.options.speedIn)
          .addClass('shown')
          .show();
        $(this.pushSelector)
          .animate({
            paddingTop: this.origHtmlMargin + (this.bannerHeight * this.scale)
          }, this.options.speedIn, 'swing', callback);
      }
      else {
        if ($.support.transition) {
          banner.animate({ top: 0 }, this.options.speedIn).addClass('shown');
          var transitionCallback = function() {
            $('html').removeClass('sb-animation');
            if (callback) {
              callback();
            }
          };
          $(this.pushSelector)
            .addClass('sb-animation')
            .one($.support.transition.end, transitionCallback)
            .emulateTransitionEnd(this.options.speedIn)
            .css('margin-top', this.origHtmlMargin + (this.bannerHeight * this.scale));
        }
        else {
          banner
            .slideDown(this.options.speedIn)
            .addClass('shown');
        }
      }
    },

    hide: function(callback) {
      var banner = $('#smartbanner');
      banner.stop();

      if (this.options.layer) {
        banner.animate({
          top: -1 * this.bannerHeight * this.scale,
          display: 'block'
        }, this.options.speedIn)
        .removeClass('shown');

        $(this.pushSelector)
          .animate({
            paddingTop: this.origHtmlMargin
          }, this.options.speedIn, 'swing', callback);
      }
      else {
        if ($.support.transition) {
          if (this.type !== 'android') {
            banner
              .css('top', -1 * this.bannerHeight * this.scale)
              .removeClass('shown');
          }
          else {
            banner
              .css({display:'none'})
              .removeClass('shown');
          }
          var transitionCallback = function() {
            $('html').removeClass('sb-animation');
            if (callback) {
              callback();
            }
          };
          $(this.pushSelector)
            .addClass('sb-animation')
            .one($.support.transition.end, transitionCallback)
            .emulateTransitionEnd(this.options.speedOut)
            .css('margin-top', this.origHtmlMargin);
        }
        else {
          banner.slideUp(this.options.speedOut).removeClass('shown');
        }
      }
    },

    close: function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      this.hide();
      this.setCookie('sb-closed', 'true', this.options.daysHidden);
      this.options.onClose(e);
    },

    install: function(e) {
      if (this.options.hideOnInstall) {
        this.hide();
      }
      this.setCookie('sb-installed', 'true', this.options.daysReminder);
      this.options.onInstall(e);
    },

    setCookie: function(name, value, exdays) {
      var exdate = new Date();
      exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays);
      value = encodeURI(value) + ((exdays == null) ? '' : '; expires=' + exdate.toUTCString());
      document.cookie = name + '=' + value + '; path=/;';
    },

    getCookie: function(name) {
      var i, x, y, ARRcookies = document.cookie.split(';');
      for (i = 0; i < ARRcookies.length; i++) {
        x = ARRcookies[i].substr(0, ARRcookies[i].indexOf('='));
        y = ARRcookies[i].substr(ARRcookies[i].indexOf('=') + 1);
        x = x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '');
        if (x == name) {
          return decodeURI(y);
        }
      }
      return null;
    },

    // Demo only.
    switchType: function() {
      var that = this;

      this.hide(function() {
        that.type = that.type == 'android' ? 'ios' : 'android';
        var meta = $(that.type == 'android' ? 'meta[name="google-play-app"]' : 'meta[name="apple-itunes-app"]').attr('content');
        that.appId = /app-id=([^\s,]+)/.exec(meta)[1];

        $('#smartbanner').detach();
        that.create();
        that.show();
      });
    }
  };

  $.smartbanner = function(option) {
    var $window = $(window);
    var data = $window.data('smartbanner');
    var options = typeof option == 'object' && option;
    if (!data) {
      $window.data('smartbanner', (data = new SmartBanner(options)));
    }
    if (typeof option == 'string') {
      data[option]();
    }
  };

  // override these globally if you like (they are all optional)
  $.smartbanner.defaults = {
    title: null, // What the title of the app should be in the banner (defaults to <title>)
    author: null, // What the author of the app should be in the banner (defaults to <meta name="author"> or hostname)
    price: 'FREE', // Price of the app
    appStoreLanguage: 'us', // Language code for App Store
    inAppStore: 'On the App Store', // Text of price for iOS
    inGooglePlay: 'In Google Play', // Text of price for Android
    inAmazonAppStore: 'In the Amazon Appstore',
    inWindowsStore: 'In the Windows Store', //Text of price for Windows
    GooglePlayParams: null, // Aditional parameters for the market
    icon: null, // The URL of the icon (defaults to <meta name="apple-touch-icon">)
    iconGloss: null, // Force gloss effect for iOS even for precomposed
    button: 'VIEW', // Text for the install button
    url: null, // The URL for the button. Keep null if you want the button to link to the app store.
    scale: 'auto', // Scale based on viewport size (set to 1 to disable)
    speedIn: 300, // Show animation speed of the banner
    speedOut: 400, // Close animation speed of the banner
    daysHidden: 15, // Duration to hide the banner after being closed (0 = always show banner)
    daysReminder: 90, // Duration to hide the banner after "VIEW" is clicked *separate from when the close button is clicked* (0 = always show banner)
    force: null, // Choose 'ios', 'android' or 'windows'. Don't do a browser check, just always show this banner
    hideOnInstall: true, // Hide the banner after "VIEW" is clicked.
    layer: false, // Display as overlay layer or slide down the page
    iOSUniversalApp: true, // If the iOS App is a universal app for both iPad and iPhone, display Smart Banner to iPad users, too.
    appendToSelector: 'body', //Append the banner to a specific selector
    pushSelector: 'html' // What element is going to push the site content down; this is where the banner append animation will start.
  };

  $.smartbanner.Constructor = SmartBanner;

  // ============================================================
  // Bootstrap transition
  // Copyright 2011-2014 Twitter, Inc.
  // Licensed under MIT (https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/blob/master/LICENSE)

  function transitionEnd () {
    var el = document.createElement('smartbanner');

    var transEndEventNames = {
      WebkitTransition: 'webkitTransitionEnd',
      MozTransition: 'transitionend',
      OTransition: 'oTransitionEnd otransitionend',
      transition: 'transitionend'
    };

    for (var name in transEndEventNames) {
      if (el.style[name] !== undefined) {
        return {end: transEndEventNames[name]};
      }
    }
    // Explicit for ie8.
    return false;
  }
  if ($.support.transition !== undefined) {
    // Prevent conflict with Twitter Bootstrap.
    return;
  }

  $(function() {
    $.support.transition = transitionEnd();
  });
  // ============================================================
});
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
